 iti sajjanānandasaṃvegajanake dīpavaṃse tatiyassa jōrj mahārañño laṅkārajja nīyyātanādi dīpanonāmekūna paññāsatimo paricchedo

 paññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
   athopi dvisahassamhitisate sattasaṭṭhime 
 sambuddhavacchare eḍvarḍbānsnāmavidito sudhī 
  
   patvā laṅkesataṃ laṅkamāga saṅkata santhavaṃ 
 sātatthamiha vāsīnaṃsarajja cirasaṇṭhitiṃ 
  
   maññamānova koḷambanagarā āmahāpurā 
 rathañjasaṃ sādhayitthavanapabbataduggame 
  
   tahiṃ yutto kiccasūroḍōsannāma mahāsayo 
 pīḷito jararogenakaḍugannāpadesake 
  
   mato tato tassamanakkāratthambhaṃ tahiṃcale 
 patiṭṭhāpayi laṅkesopuna kaḷyāṇisindhuyaṃ 
  
   ṭhapāpayī doṇisetuṃmahāvaṇṇusavantiyā 
 mahāsetuṃ dārumayaṃkārāpayi yathārahaṃ 
  
   rammaṃ päviliyannāmamandiraṃ nayanussavaṃ 
 sirivaḍḍhanaṭhānīyekārāpayi vicitrakaṃ 
  
   pāsāṇakacchadesasmiṃratanākarasantike 
 mavunṭläviniyānāmaṃrammaṃ dhanaparibbayā 
  
   pāsādaṃ kārayi pacchānayisvasanasālataṃ 
 tappadesampi tannāmāvoharanti videsikā 
  
    
 laṅkeso paṭhamaṃ laṅkāvāsīnaṃ gaṇanaṃ tadā 
 gaṇāpayi sātirekaṃbhavi sāddhaṭhalakkhakaṃ 
  
    
 samayesmiṃ jōrjbarḍnāmogaṅgāsiripurantike 
 sīhapiṭṭhipadesamhikopivatthuṃ vapāpayī 
  
    
 tabbappakānaṃ laṅkesobahavo bhūpadesake 
 phātikkattuṃ laṅkamimaṃnimmūlena pavecchi so 
  
    
 iṃgīrasijanatā tasmiṃkāle mahāparissamā 
 nagarālokavikhyātapadesaṃ pariyesayuṃ 
  
    
 tato paṭṭhāya taṃ desaṃsukhassitaṃ sukhatthikā 
 sakalā jātiyā yantipativassaṃ mahaddhanā

 gamanāgamane tamhiphāsuyā pāṇinaṃ bhusaṃ 
 sodhāpayī mahāmaggaṃmaggāmaggavisārado 
  
    
 tadeva koḷambapurepaṭhamaṃ bahikoṭṭhake 
 potthakāvāsamakaruṃnānāpotthakasaṅkulaṃ 
  
    
 tado parima raṭṭhasmimiṃgīrasibalavattane 
 yo samussahi saṅgāmavijayakkamakovido 
  
    
 sajōnḍoyilnāmakhyātomantīso thirabuddhimā 
 seṅkhaṇḍaselanagaremaccurājavasaṅgato 
  
    
 nimujjāpiya nārīnamudake sasanaṃ pati 
 purāsīhalarājūnaṃyā nīti taṃ pariccaji 
  
    
 ähäḷēpolavikhyātomahāmaccaggasīhalo 
 mato murisiyasnāmadīpasmiṃ dukkhito tadā 
  
    
 saramānā guṇaṃlaṅkāpatibimbaṃ sarūpimaṃ 
 ṭhapesuṃ koḷambapurerājamandirasammukhe 
  
    
 pasādetvāna laṅkesolaṅkādīpanivāsino 
 sakadesaṅgami sattavassaṃvasitvihānagho 
  
    
 dvisahasse tisatasmiṃcatusattatime jine 
 saṃvacchare roborṭvilmaṭhōrṭannāmasuvissuto 
  
    
 pappuyya laṅkissarattamihāga karuṇāparo 
 laṅkesosi dhuvaṃ dīpavāsīnaṃ hitasādhako 
  
    
 rajjesmiṃ paṭhamaṃ sēviṃsnāmena pākaṭaṃ tadā 
 mūlālayañcārabhiṃsujanānaṃ vuddhikāmato 
  
    
 pavattijānane aññamaññassa phāsuyā bhusaṃ 
 lekhane pesituṃ sīghaṃkoḷambapurato tadā 
  
    
 yāvaseṅkhaṇḍaselavhapuraṃ paṭṭhapayī rathaṃ 
 heṭṭhāraṭṭhe landajanāyonakadamiḷesu hi 
  
    
 bhūbhāgānamadānasmiṃkāretuṃ mandire thire 
 paññāpayiṃsu yaṃ nītiṃpaṭikkhipiya sabbaso

 gehe kārayituṃ sammābhūbhāgedāsi mūlato

 purāmarammavisayaṃgatena yatisāminā 
 saddhiṃ puna bodhigacchapiṭṭhigāmubbhavo guṇi 
  
    
 dhammajotisāmaṇerodhammasatthesu pesalo 
 mahāvidānamudalippamukhānaṃ nivediya 
  
    
 laddhopakāraṃ amarapuraṃ gantvāna saṅayā 
 suvaṇṇaguhapaññātāsīmāyamupasampadaṃ

 labhitvā dhammavinayaṃsammuggayhāsihāgato 
  
    
 dhammajjotiyatindo sovinayaññū visārado 
 dvisahasse tisatasmiṃpañca sattatime jine

 paṭṭhapitthāmarapuranikāyaṃ sabbhi vaṇṇitaṃ 
  
    
 kālessa laṅkāpatinokalambujanaraliti 
 pavattipattamiṃgīrasibhāsāya susamārabhuṃ 
  
    
 rajje seṭṭhadhurandhārīmantīhirabhitaṃ tahaṃ dosānamadhirajjamhipākaṭattā nivāritaṃ 
  
    
 rajjaṃ pālayituṃ sammānītisampādikā tathā 
 nītividhāyikādvehasabhārabhi tadaddhaniva 
  
    
 dhurīhi paṭhamā yuttāsabhā navahi mantihi 
 chahevā dhurimantihilaṅkesena samaṃbhavi 
  
    
 vidhāyikā ca dutiyāsabhā navahi mantihi 
 yuttā dhurīhi mantīhilaṅkesena samaṃbhavi 
  
    
 pubbuttarā pacchimā camajjhimādakkhiṇā iti 
 vibhattā pañcadhā laṅkālaṅkādhīsena dhīmatā

 niyojayittha laṅkindoniyoga nipuṇo guṇi

 nānādesesu ṭhapayīsālā tannāmikā thiraṃ

 tannāmiko ca sacivomanti dunuvilavhayo

 vibhattā pañcadhā laṅkālaṅkādhīsena dhīmatā

 tathā katipayā mantīyatayo ca tayotime 
 sirivikkamādi rājasīharājassa kassaci 
  
    
 bandhussopariraṭṭhasmiṃrajjaṃ pavārituṃ tadā 
 kumantayiṃsu taṃ ñatvārājakiccamhi tapparo

 gāhāpayitvā seṭṭhādhikaraṇaṃ nesi buddhimā

 disāpatidhuraṃdāsicatuyojanaraṭṭhake

 esiyātikavikhyātāsabhāraddhāsi sādhuhi 
  
    
 ambarukkhārāmanāmevihāredhissaro guṇī 
 laṅkāsaṃsuddhasambuddhasāsanambara bhāsuro 
  
    
 sasīva ñāṇavimalatissanāmena vissuto

 vikṭōriyānāmasutākumārī kāminī piyā 
 samayasmiṃdhirajjesmiṃrājinīsi tathāviha

 ketavaṃ sabbaso nītimaggeneva paṭikkhipi

 koḷambapurato yāvagālunagaramantare

 uggaṇhāpayituṃ tesaṃpāṭhasālā ṭhapāpayī

 laṅkāvāsābhilāsaṃ sohitvāḍḍhuḍḍhasamaṃ sudhī

 vasittha ce thoka kālaṃbahukiccāni kārayi

 tisate caturāsītimite sambuddhahāyane

 katvā padesaṃ vibhajivāyavoti yathārahaṃ 
  
    
 yāvalaṅkissaramimaṃpariraṭṭhe pavattitaṃ 
 dāsavyaṃ vāritaṃ nītimaggeniha visesato

 yatisīho kaviketupūtakittidayālayo

 samārabhitvā lokatthasiddhiṅkāsasmimaddhani

 pāpetuṃ satthasadanaṃvidhimantaṃrabhiṃsaviha

 chabbassamiha ṭhitvānatasmiṃ yāte sadesakaṃ 
 dvisahasse tisatasmiṃnavutime munivacchare

 laṅkādīpādhivāsīnaṃvavaḍḍhenteappasādake

 tadappasannā janatājanayuṃ kalahaṃ lahuṃ

 yuddhanītiṃ pakāsetvāmādhurānayi vāhinī

 bhayato tajjitā sīghaṃkalahampi nivattayuṃ

 nītibbidū mahāmaccāhūya laṅkissaraṃ tadā

 dhurāpetuṃ sassa lahuṃnivedayiṃsu taṅkhaṇe

 ekapaññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
   gate tasmiṃ dvisahassetisate tinavutime 
 munindasaradasmiṃ jōrjänḍarsannāmavissuto 
  
   patvā laṅkesattamāgarajje dhanaparikkhayaṃ 
 samecca dhanavuddhiṃ sokattuṃ maññi nakāriye 
  
   anārambhe dhūmarathamaggassa sahasā idha 
 laṅkissare appasannāvappakā ca videsikā 
   thāmaṃ sāmaggiyā sīghaṃdīpetumārabhuṃ sabhaṃ 
 laṅkindassa lahuṃ tassāsabhāya cāsumaggalā 
  
   bhūrīparādhahetuttāmajjhime visaye tadā 
 surālayāpanītāsuṃbahavo hitakāmato 
  
   tasseva tatiye vassepattaṃ paṭissavaṃ pabhū 
 asallakkhiya rajjenagopitaṃ radadhātukaṃ 
  
   pahāya rajja sambandhapupphārāmādhivāsino 
 netussa cassaselavhavihāredhissarassa ca 
  
   yatindassa tathā nīravaḍḍhakassa ca mantino 
 pavāresabuddhabhattojahi sāsanarakkhaṇaṃ 
  
   laṅkeso pañcavassānivasitvana yathāruci 
 sadesaṅgami laṅkātopeto sopetanuddayo 
  
    
 henrīvōḍsnāmavikhyātolaṅkesotha sadāsayo 
 dvisahassattisataṭṭhanavutime jinahāyane

 kicce kārayituṃ sīghaṃrabhi sūro visārado 
  
    
 soyaṃ laṅkissaro dhīmāyānāyāne sukhatthiko 
 tadāni setuyo maggekārāpayi dayāparo 
  
    
 koḷambaseṅkhaṇḍaselappurānamantare thiraṃ 
 sādhetuṃ duggame dhīromahā dhūma rathañjasaṃ

 gaṅgāsiripure kaṇṭagacchatitthappadesake

 teladoṇivhayasmiṃ cahintālopalagāmake

 laddhā mrammanikāyasmiṃpabbajjaṃ dvīhi bhikkhuhi

 hitvānajjhāpanaṃ nāmabhāgaṃ vibhaji rajjato

 mahānetā mahāvyattodhammādhāravhavissuto

 tadā pākatikaṅkaṃsurajjato yodhadigghikaṃ 
  
    
 mantanassabhatiṃ nītidāyikāyoddharaṭṭhake 
 mantidhuraṃ sīhalānamekaṃ ṭhapesi buddhimā 
  
    
 tatheva laṅkissaro somāhammadikajātinaṃ 
 pādāsyekaṃ mantidhuraṃkāruññaparamo tadā 
  
    
 majjhimāsāya sabaraggāmāseti visuṃ disaṃ 
 katvāna tassaṃ ratanapuraṃ mukhyapuraṅkari 
  
  sl            
  
    
 tadeva devanagaratitthe dīpālaye subhe 
 jotāpayittha paṭhamaṃpajjotaṃ kittijotimā 
  
    
 laṅkeso kasiyā vuddhimapekkhesomhi dīpake 
 vivarittha kasikammavijjāgāraṃ guṇālayo 
  
    
 naṭṭhāvasiṭṭhe kammanteporāṇe rakkhituṃ idha 
 purāvijjārakkhakātiṭhapesi kārakaṃ sabhaṃ 
  
    
 mahesino sāsanavuddhisambhavaṃ 
 samicchamānā janatā suvissutā 
 samecca bhatyā sugatādisāsano 
 dayābhidhānaṃ pariveṇamārabhuṃ 
  
    
 tahaṃdhipaccūpagatodimo dhiyā 
 kavi ssutejena ravī muduttayā 
 sasi tthiraddi vimalādisāradhi 
 patī virocitthiha satthabhāsato 
  
    
 sadesadesantarasamphuṭāriya 
 ssilokanādo kaviketuvissuto 
 mahāgaṇī tappariveṇamaggato 
 mahatthasiddhiṅkari sādhu pāṇinaṃ 
  
    
 vasiha paramaviññāṇatthanāmassabhāya 
 madhipati bhaviyatthaṃ vīsavassappamāṇaṃ 
 sumariya parisāyaṃ tāya ārēmiranda 
 viditadhivacano so buddhimā vuddhikāmo 
  
    
 suvisadatatakittī ñātasatthāgamādi 
 viracayi varasīmālakkhaṇaddīpatiṃ yo 
 varakavitilako so vissutosseva kāle 
 paravavimalasārattheranetā divaṅgā 
  
    
 iha janahitakārī santataṃ sattajāta 
 manakamalavanaṃ yo bodhayī laṅkadhīso 
 gaditayasaninādo khyātagōrḍansamañño 
 sudhi gami sakadesaṃ sattavassaṃ vasitvā 
  
 bhāṇavāraṃ tipaññāsatimaṃ 
  
 iti sajjanānanda saṃvega janake dīpavaṃse laṅkesattaya dīpano nāma 
 tepaññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
  sl            
  
 catupaññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
   atha vigatavatīto tamhi laṅkāpatismiṃ 
 catusatacatutiṃsādhikyake dvissahasse 
 naravarasaradasmiṃ mañjulaṅkaṃ hi hävlok 
 viditadhivacanopāgañchi laṅkissareso 
  
   dayamuduhadayo so desatāṇakkamasmiṃ 
 paṭutaramatimāsmiṃ dīpake vattamānaṃ 
 janagaṇaparimāṇaṃ tassa kālepi pubbe 
 yathariva pariñātuṃ saṅgaṇāpesi dhīmā 
  
   narapatisamayasmiṃ vattitaṃ vīhisuṅka 
 gahaṇamanucitanti manti jōrjvōl samañño 
 sumariya varamedho dunnayaṃ tañhi nītiṃ 
 apanayi janaphātiṅkāmi laṅkissarena 
  
   tadapiriha janānaṃ vuddhimākaṅkhamānā 
 rabhi suviditamaggaṃ ṭäknikalsatthasālaṃ 
 pavaraparamaviññāṇatthasaññasabhāto 
 sanikamakarirambhaṃnandavijjālayaggā 
  
   surasuravaravāṇīccantacheko sañāṇa 
 tilakayatipatīso bhāratīyā vibhāvī 
 iha suviditavijjobhāsasatthālayaggaṃ 
 janagaṇahitakāmī sārabhi tamhi kāle 
  
   janahitanirate so kantakaḷyāṇinajjaṃ 
 atisayaputhusetuṃ khyātavikṭōriyavhaṃ 
 tathariva sakanāmiṃnāmayāgāramuccā 
 yatamatirucihävlokpākaṭaṅkārayittha 
  
   sudhivaraguṇasālī laṅkadhīso sadhūma 
 rathapathamatidīghaṃ kārayīhāsu sammā 
 vasiyiha sarade so pañca hävloksamañño 
 apagami sakadesaṃ pīnayaṃ pāṇipūgaṃ 
  
  sl            
  
   atisayasutalaṅkādhissarasmiṃ payāte 
 suvisada yasanādo rijvenāmo sirīmā 
 imamupagami laṅkaṃ patva laṅkissarattaṃ caturatarakathī so buddhimā suddhabuddhyā 
  
   subhataravaralaṅkaṃ phātikattuṃbhilāso 
 vividhapacuradhaññuppattihetukirayāto 
 bahutaradhanavuddhi sādhuvassāpayanto 
 iha jananikaraṃ santosayī santataṃva 
  
    
 tadiha pabhujanā sambhattiyā sogatābya 
 suvi suta pariveṇaṃ saddhikā sārabhiṃsu 
 suviditasirisādimaṅgalavherugāme 
 tahamadhi patirāsādisaṃnetā vibhāvī 
  
    
 tidivamupagatasmiṃ tamhidhīse kavīse 
 viditasamayasattho ganthakattā pavīṇo 
 tahamadhipatibhāvaṃ patva dhīmā sañāṇa 
 vimalasutayatindo satthalokaṃ karittha 
  
    
 tadapiha matasattho sikkhito buddhadhamme 
 sunisitamati seṭṭho indajotī yatīnaṃ 
 labhiya janagaṇānaṃjjhesanaṃ kovido pā 
 vacanudayasamaññaṃ satthasālaṃrabhittha 
  
    
 visadayasaninādo tassa kālamhi dhamma 
 ratana yatipatindo dhammasatthappavīṇo 
 suvidita pariveṇaṃnandanāmaṃrabhitvā 
 pavarataramatīyākāsi lokatthasiddhiṃ 
  
    
 iha suviditakaḷyāṇīrudesamhi kante 
 tathariva sutayāpāpaṭṭanaṭṭhāniyamhi 
 avitaruciralaṅkassassa kālamhi dhūma 
 rathapathakaraṇañcāsuṃrabhiṃsūdha rajjā 
  
    
 pacurapavaravīthipaṇyasālābhi citre 
 ruciratarapurasmiṃ khyātakoḷambasaññe 
 nikhilajanasukhatthaṃ kārayī sādhu vijju 
 rathagamanamudāyaṃ sā bavusṭarḍsamajjā 
  
  sl            
  
    vividhajanapapuṇṇe kantakoḷambanāme 
 viditapuravarasmiṃ hārititthe padhāne 
 varataraṇitaḷākaṃ kātave maññamāno 
 nikhani paṭhamapaṃsūpuñjakaṃ laṅkadhiso 
  
    
 vipuladharaṇibhāraṃ sārahāraṃ vahantī 
 tatasuvisadakittīvallivindussa lekhā 
 nikhilahadayahārī khyātavikṭōriyavhā 
 upagami samayesmiṃ rājinī maccurājaṃ 
  
    
 itupagatavatīyā nāmasesaṃ hi tāyaṃ 
 pavaravidhiniyogāhādhirajje ca tassā 
 pamukhapavarasūnu sattamoḍvarḍsamañño 
 thiramatiguṇavāso so mahābhūpatīsi 
  
    
 labhiya varaniyogaṃ tātarañño vidhīmā 
 piyataravaralaṅkaṃ daṭṭhukāmomhi kāle 
 upagami dhitimāsmiṃ vēlskumāro variṭṭho 
 sapadiha paṭigaṇhī sādhukaṃ pāṇirāsī 
  
    
 tadiha janagaṇānaṃ satthapāguññakāmā 
 rabhumuda sutanōrmannāmavijjālayaggaṃ 
 nayanagadavināsāyaggavikṭōriyavhaṃ 
 ṭhapayī tadapi kātuṃrogya sālaṃdimasmiṃ 
  
    
 amarapuranivāsī saddhikā vittasāmī 
 sukhacitamaṇimuttābhāsuraṃ sundaraṃva 
 kanakamayakaraṇḍaṃdāya laṅkaṃ gamitvā 
 munivararadadhātuṃ pūjayuṃ tena bhatyā 
  
    
 viditasamayasattho sīlanandābhidhāno 
 yatipatiriha saddhammākarākhyaṃpasiddhaṃ 
 varamati pariveṇaṃ sādhubhāvārabhitvā 
 akari sucirakālaṃ sāsanapphātimaggaṃ 
  
    
 naravaravarapāṇī saṅgamitvā tadāni 
 samudayamabhilāsī sāsanaṅgī rasassa 
 paramataruṇabuddhassaṃsadaṃ sārabhiṃsu 
 sahi janahitasāraṃ sādhayatyajja yāva 
  
  sl            
  
    
 yamakari varacetyaṃ kākavaṇṇāditissaviditadharaṇipālo sādhu tissorurāme 
 atisayaviriyeko sāmaṇero hi sabbhi 
 saha kira paṭisaṅkhārāpayappaṃ vinaṭṭhaṃ 
  
    
 punarapi aparesmiṃ maccuvāsaṃ payāte 
 ṭhapiya samitimaggaṃ cetyavuddhiṃ padhānā 
 labhiya sadupakāraṃ sogatānaṃ pahūtaṃ 
 puthutaradhitiyā taṃ sādhu niṭṭhāpayiṃsu 
  
    
 samudayamiha pācīnaggabhāsānamicchaṃ 
 varamati samayesmiṃjjhāpanajjhakkhakohi 
 vidurajanacayaṃ sonetva mantetva sammā 
 rabhi vara samitiṃ pācīnabhāsopakāraṃ 
  
    
 tahamadhipatitaṃ es em barōsnāmakhyāto 
 matisacivavaropāgamma so lekhakattaṃ 
 dadiya sutaguṇādivaḍḍhanākhyassudhissa 
 saradamanu parikkhaṃ sārabhī māgadhādiṃ 
  
    
 tathariva sudhi hārvarḍnāmamantissaro ca 
 matisacivavariṭṭho khyātaḍenhemsamañño 
 sacivadhipati mäkrenāmikojjhakkhakā te 
 sabhatimadhipatittaṃ patva vuddhiṅkariṃsu 
  
    
 vidurajanavirāje saṃsadesmiṃ tato hi 
 paramatimatimā ē em guṇassekharākhyo 
 guṇaratanabhidhāno so häraḍpubbikova 
 sudhitasutamudalindā pālayuṃ lekhakattaṃ 
  
    
 tahamadhipatidāni sorobinsansamañño 
 matisacivavaro tabbuddhisiddhiṅkareyya 
 thiramatiguṇavā ī ēbhayassekharākhyo 
 vahati samudalindo lekhakattaṃ hi tassaṃ 
  
    
 varakavicayarājikārakākhyassabhāya 
 sahitasutasamajjā satthakāmīnamatthaṃ 
 satatamanibhamaggaṃ sādhayantītimattaṃ 
 vilasatiriha dīpenītikā yāvaajja 
  
  sl            
  
    
 munisamayabhivuddhiṃpekkhamānā tadevā 
 rabhumuda sutavijjānandavijjālayaggaṃ 
 tahamadhipatibhāvaṃ patva dhammādirāmā 
 dhivacanathavireso satthalokaṅkarittha 
  
    
 vividhavidhividhānā dīpamaggaṃ samiddhaṃ 
 kariyidha dhuvasāraṇīyavutti pajāhi 
 sudhiguṇanīdhibhūto rijvenāmo salaṅkā 
 dhipati gami sadesaṃ ettha vasseṭṭha ṭhitvā 
  
    atha piyaguṇayutto blēksamañño hi laṅkā 
 dhipatitamupagantvā pāpuṇī dvissahasse 
 sacatusatachatāḷīsādhike buddhavasse 
 paramamihabhivuddhiṃ cintayantotimattaṃ 
  
    
 pabhujanagaṇamānetvāna bhatyā samukhyo 
 kasikiriyasabhaṃ sammārabhīnuddayālū 
 ṭhapitakasisamajjāmaggatosmiṃ hi dīpe 
 pacuratarasadattho sambhavī bhāvamāno 
  
    
 sahi nagaravarasmiṃ seṭṭhatitthe manuññaṃ 
 varataraṇitaḷākaṃ cāyatā tuṅgamaggaṃ 
 atisaya piyanettārogyasālaṃ visālaṃ 
 vivari manujajāte pītimāvedayante 
  
    
 bhuvi tatarucikittī buddhimā suddhaceto 
 suviditavaracūḷālaṅkatisyāmarājā 
 samupagamiya laṅkaṃ desacāro tadeva 
 ihadhipatipadhānā sesasammānitova 
  
    
 sakamudupadadhūlīpūtalokesasakka 
 narapatimakuṭassaggaññadhammassuphassaṃ 
 alabhi dasanadhātu yā munindassa taṃva 
 namitumahitukāmogā mahāṭhāniyaggaṃ 
  
    
  
 tahamavanipatindodiccabandhussa tibba 
 suvisadaradadhātuṃ disva natvā mahitvā 
 pavarasuthirabhatyā phassituṃ pāṇinā taṃ 
 asamayasamayācī tāyake taṃ pasanno 
  
  sl            
  
    
 api ca vidita vārīvaḍḍhanakhyātamantī 
 nadadi kamavirodhantīha vatvakkamaññū 
 atha narapatiseṭṭho rosavessānarena 
 atisayajalamānopāgamī dhātugehā 
  
    
 rucirapavaralaṅkāmātupāmokkhasūnu 
 sajanahitabhilāsī sūravīro nibhīto 
 iha jananayanehī mocayaṃsū tadā jōn 
 kotalāvalabhidhāno pañcataṃ manti yāto 
  
    
 munivacanapathasmiṃ sikkhito satthavedī 
 riha suvidita dhammārāma thero yatindo 
 varamati pariveṇaṃ taṃ hi vijjādibandhuṃ 
 rabhiyadhipati tasmiṃ sādhayaṃ bhāsiyatthaṃ 
  
    
 sirimati sirilaṅkādhissare blēksamaññe 
 gatavati catuvassaṃ ṭhitvito sassa desaṃ 
 samacatusatapaññāsādhike dvisahasse 
 sirighasaradasmiṃ henrimäklamsamavho 
  
    
 upagami sirilaṅkādhissaro bhūya dhīmā 
 idha janasamavuttī mantanassaṃsadaṃ so 
 mahipavaraniyogākādhirajje visesaṃ 
 tadapi pavaradīpe vāsinaṃ vuddhiyāsi 
  
    
 dasasu viditamantisvettha vāsīnachandā 
 supaṭitacatumantī uccinetuṃvakāsaṃ 
 ṭhapayī catusu tesviṃgīrasinaṃ dve ca mantī 
 tathariva aparekolandiyānañca manti 
  
    
 nivasatamiha dosaññūnameko ca mantī 
 bhavumiti catumantī channamaññesameko 
 uparimavijitamhā mantiko heṭṭharaṭṭhā 
 aparapavaramantī dve sudaṃ sīhalānaṃ 
    
 tathariva damiḷānaṃ dve ca mantīdha muslim 
 iti viditajanānaṃ cekamantītichete 
 tadiha matimatā laṅkādhinā pāpitāsuṃ 
 pavaradhuradadhānekārasāsuṃ ca mantī 
  
  sl             
  
    
 vasumatiparakittīpatthivāsannikāsa 
 dayavisadasiloko buddhimā sāmakāmo 
 mahipati sutaäḍvarḍsavhayo sattamo so 
 gamiriha samayasmiṃ kittisesattanaṃhi 
  
    
 puna sutagarurajje rājino tassa seṭṭha 
 piyataratanayo so pañcamo jōrj samañño 
 sudhivaraguṇasaṅgo muttikittī samāno 
 vidhiniyamavasā sīhāsanāsīnakosī 
  
    
 valahagoḍasamañño devavāsosi gaṅgā 
 sirinagaravarasmiṃ tatu devālayasmiṃ 
 patisamamanaghampyāsāḷhikaṃ pāṭihīraṃ 
 pacurajanasametā sīhalaṃ vattayanti 
  
    
 tathariva ciravāsī yonakā tamhi gaṅgā 
 siripurapavarasmiṃ kārayuṃ pallimekaṃ 
 tahamatha samayesmiṃ dibbavāse purāva 
 hanati turiyabherī palliñattā manuññā 
  
    
 vajati nadisakāsaṃ pāṭihīre manāpe 
 mahamadikajanā tappallisāmantakasmiṃ 
 turiyahananamāsuṃ vāraṇīyantyavocuṃ 
 tahamatisamitattā sogatā vimbhitāva 
  
    
 akariya kalahaṃ taṃ majjhimāsāpatissa 
 surasadanadhikārī vedayī abbhutatthaṃ 
 sahimahamadikānaṃ pakkhapātī bhavitvā 
 tahamatha turiyānaṃ vādanaṃ vārayittha 
  
    
 puna siranilayādhikāri mantī tamatthaṃ 
 anayadhikaraṇaṃ seṅkhaṇḍaselappurasmiṃ 
 sunisitanayavedī nicchayakkāraseṭṭho 
 samanugamiya pubbiṃ taṃ paṭiññañca pattaṃ 
  
    
 tamadhīkaraṇamaggaṃ samparikkhitva sīghaṃ 
 nayamanuda disādhīsassa kāmaṃ vipakkhaṃ 
 puthumativaramantī pōl i pīris samañño 
 visadamakari seṭṭhaṃ nicchayaṃ nītidakkho 
  sl            
    
 tadapi asahamāno majjhimāsādhipo so 
 pavaradhikaraṇaṃtaṃ netva tamhā sapakkhaṃ 
 kathampi labhi tuṇṇaṃ tiraṇaṃ aññadāni 
 samathamanayi bādhaṃ laṅkadhīsonukampo 
  
    
 suviditasurabhāso māgadhādo pavīṇo 
 kavi siririyavaṃsakhyātanetāmhi kāle 
 pabhujananikarenārādhito maṅgalākhyaṃ 
 rabhiriha pariveṇaṃdhissaro bhūya bhāti 
  
    
 jinajanasamudāyo yaṃ parakkantibāhuṃ 
 rabhi sutapariveṇaṃdhissaro tamhi netā 
 sirijinaratanavho therasīho yasassī 
 vipulatarasadatthaṅkāsi tammaggatova 
  
    
 punariha sirilaṅkeso surāsuṅkanītiṃ 
 ṭhapayī pahari setūsuṅkagāhaṃ tadāni 
 adhikamakari nāvānītadabbānasuṅkaṃ 
 tadapi nikhilalaṅkādassanañcābhavittha 
  
    
 katiriti samayesmiṃ pāṇayo laṅkadhīso 
 avagamitumapekko saṅgaṇāpesi satte 
 tadapi kiriyamāsuṃ niṭṭhapetvāna dhūma 
 rathagamanamakāresāmadhuggāmamādo 
  
    
 viditapuravarasmiṃ kantakoḷambanāme 
 sukhanitaparakāle bērenāme taḷāke 
 atisayaviriyaṃsaṃ pūrayī paṃsunājja 
 varagharavisikhāyo dissare mālinīva 
  
    
 munisamayudayesi sādhu muddā 
 payitumudaṭṭhakathā rabhittha tantyaṃ 
 sakavipuladhanabbayā sahēvā 
 vitaraṇiyo sayimansamaññamanti 
  
    
 ghanatimisavidhaṃsi raṃsimālī 
 ravisadiso tanayittha satthalokaṃ 
 suvitatavarakitti desadese 
 sasirisumaṅgalanetusāmipādo 
  
  sl            
  
    
 viditapavarasatthabhāvavijjo 
 dayapariveṇadhipo mahāvibhāvī 
 gami divamamarānasāsituṃva dharaṇitalaṃ timiraṃ tatobhavittha 
  
    
 anunayamanisaṃ hi pālya laṅkaṃ 
 jananikaraṃ pihayaṃ hi pañcavassaṃ 
 sahadhikamiha ṭhitvagañchi mäklam 
 viditabhidho vijitaṃsa laṅkadhīso 
  
    
 varakavivisarā patitakittī 
 garumahipā dhaninokhileva kāmaṃ 
 sakasakatanuyo pahāyagañchūṃ 
 kimuta paresamanantadaṅkuruvho 
  
 bhāṇavāraṃ catupaññāsatimaṃ 
  
 iti sajjanānanda saṃvega janake dīpavaṃse catulaṅkesa dīpano nāma 
 catupaññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
  sl            
  
 pañcapaññāsatimo paricchedo  
  
   dvisahassaccatusatachapaññāsamite jine laṅkissaro roborṭcāmarssamaññosi idhāgato 
  
   so kho munindasamayaṃbhāsaṃ māgadhikaṃ tathā 
 pākaṭosi vijaññātibhāsantaravisārado 
  
   teneva sogatā sabbetassehāgamanaṃ pati 
 bhīyyo pasannā sammodavācamavedayuṃ tadā 
  
   tasseva laṅkāpatinokāle koḷambaṭhāniye vicarittha cāmarsdhaññāgāraṃ sammodamānaso 
  
   purā laṅkāyamāraddhoyāvasindhupadesakaṃ 
 sādhetvāna dhūmarathamaggo niṭṭhāpito tadā 
  
   vyatto so pālibhāsāyatabbuddhikāmato bhusaṃ 
 majjhimaṭṭhakathaṃ seṭṭhaṃpapañcasūdanissutaṃ 
  
   pariveṇedhipatināvijjālaṅkāravissute 
 dhammasatthappavīṇenabhāsantara vijānatā 
  
   dhammārāmasamaññenayatindena vipassinā 
 sodhāpetvāna sahasāmuddāpayi yathākkamaṃ 
  
   tatheva kāleparasmiṃjātakaṭṭhakathaṃriyaṃ 
 iṃgīrasibhāsāya mudāparivattiya so budho 
  
    
 eṅgalantamahādīpemahaddhanaparibbayā 
 muddāpetvāna sambhatyātanayittha sadāsayo 
  
    
 byattosi cepi kusalobhāsāsatthavisārado 
 tasseva kāle lokopivipattimukhamāgami 
  
    
 jarmanpraṃsaitikhyātavaṃsikesu mahāhavo 
 sudussaho bhūrisattaghātako cāsi sabbaso 
  
    
 vattamāne raṇe tamhirajjameṃglantanāmikaṃ 
 samaggahī pransapakkhaṃsāhāyyena lahuṃ tadā 
  
    
 saṅkulasseva yuddhassalaṅkātova mahaddhanaṃ 
 tatheva raṇasūre capesayuṃglantarajjakaṃ 
  
    
 dhanahāniṃ janahāniṃraṭṭhahāniṃ savāhini 
 anapekkhiya yujjhiṃsusamūpabbūḷhakā bhusaṃ 
  
  sl            
  
    
 pavattite catuvassaṃtasmiṃ saṅkula saṃyuge 
 jarmannāmā jātikā teparājiṃsvatha taṃ samī 
  
    
 mahāsaṃyugakālamhilaṅkāyañca bhayānakaṃ 
 bhaṇḍanaṃsi sīhalīyayonakānaṃnapekkhitaṃ 
  
    
 sabbattha sabbadā sabbesogatā pativaccharaṃ 
 vesākhussavamaccantaṃpavattentīha pītiyā 
  
    
 dvisahasse catusatekūnasaṭṭhimahāyane 
 vesākhapuṇṇamadinesogatānaṃ mahāmahe 
  
    
 seṅkhaṇḍaselanagarevattamāne tadussave 
 tato tato chaṇaṃ daṭṭhuṃjanakāyā samosaṭā 
  
    
 sambuddhamāmakā sesāradadhātuṃ namassiya

 ḍī bī  jayādītilako sirīmā 
 kavī sabhānāyakataṃ sadesa 
 kattabbahāraṃ sacivattanañca

    so bhāgyavā vikkamasālivyatta 
 kittī purā vaṇṇitanāmadheyyo 
 kannaṅgaro mantivaro idāni 
 ajjhāpanāmaccadhuraṃ dadhāti 
  
    
 dhanī guṇī vissūtakitti ḍī es  
 senādinetā janatā hitesi

 liv ār  ḍayasbaṇḍaranāyakākhyo 
 sudhī disāpālakamaccaṭhāna 
 ntaraṃ dadhāti susucheka mantī 
  
    
 kirayāpavīṇo sudhi kammakāra 
 vāṇijjamaccappadaviṃ pasiddho 
 ji sī  esādī korayā bhidhāno 
 dadhāti mantī taruṇo surūpo 
  
    
 sadeva jātyāgamabhattiyutto 
 cirantanabbuttivido vidhiññū

 maccappadaṃ saṃvidadhe vidhiññū

 ṭiralsamañño sacivo matīmā 
 laṅkāmahālekhadhuraṃ vahitvā 
 vissāmataṃ patva agā sadesaṃ

 dayaddaceto paricinnalaṅko 
 em em  väḍarbanvidito sajīvo 
 laṅkāmahālekhadhuraṃ dadhāti 
  
  sl            
  
    
 pāmokkhakodhīkaraṇamhi jē sī  
 hōvarḍsamañño sacivosi dhīmā 
 hakshämsamavho satimā sabhaṇḍā 
 gārīyamaccappadaviṃ dadhāti 
  
    
 tayo cimemaccavarā pasiddhā 
 dhurandharā chekatarā bhaviṃsu 
 yathāpurā vuttasabhā tatheva 
 sabbaṅgapuṇṇā vitathā nasesā 
  
    
 samattavanyaṃ visadekakitti 
 ppabhāvamaggaṃ tanayittha yo so 
 bhūmissaro pañcamajōrjsamañño 
 mahādayo sassa pajāsu daḷhaṃ 
  
    
 kālessa laṅkāpatino sakīye 
 santāpayaṃ suddhayasottabhāvaṃ

 dhattuṃvagañchi bhuvanaṃ parampi

 sabandhavo dukkhamanā yathāsuṃ 
 sasāmibhattā katavedinotra 
 dīpe janāccantadukhā rudiṃsu 
  
    
 tato sato jōrjmahipassa jeṭṭha 
 suto patīto piyavēlskumāro 
 dayodapūtaggamanoṭṭhameḍvarḍ 
 nāmena sīhāsanasīnakosi 
  
    
 navodayaṃ vatrabhuno dhajassa 
 viyassa bhūpassa sato vipassī 
 samattasattonnayanā sakīyā 
 nandiṃsu hīyyo taguṇe vadantā 
  
    
 eḍvarḍmahābhūpatisattajātaṃ 
 samonavassaṃ paritosayitvā 
 pakāsayaṃ bhāgasabhāvamagga 
 rajjassa bhāraṃ jahi kenacīva 
  
  sl            
  
    
 atho sagabbho mahipassa tassa 
 yōkādipādo vidhinā sunīto 
 chaṭṭhena jōrjkhyātabhidhena sīhā 
 sanamhisīno janatā hitāya 
  
    
 patiṭṭhitaṃ taṃ puna ādipādaṃ 
 rajje nisammaññadisampatīnaṃ 
 purā bhusaṃ cetasi dhūmitova 
 hutāvahosīva samuṭṭhito hi

 mahāmahīposi yatheva kante 
 laṅkaggarajjepi disampatī so 
 rājākhilānaṃ lasataṃ hitāya 
  
    
 vijjodayākhyassutasatthasālo 
 dayācalabbhūtasusattharaṃsī

 visiṭṭhadhamme nipuṇo marūnaṃ 
 bhidhammamāsuṃ vadituṃva dhīmā 
 devādinando garusaṅghaneto 
 pasaṅgarājā gami devalokaṃ

 seṅkhaṇḍaselavhapure varasmiṃ 
 pupphādirāmādhipatī yasassī 
 sumaṅgalavho garunetupādo 
  
    
 ramme vihāre hayaselasañño 
 dhīso purasmiṃ sirivaḍḍhanākhye 
 guṇī guṇādīratano samullē 
 gāmubbhavo netuvaro vibhāti 
  
    
 saddhammasatthe paṭu saṅgharāja 
 satthālayasmiṃdhipatīnunetā 
 siddhatthanāmo thaviro matīmā 
 virājate sāsanavuddhikāmī 
  
  sl            
  
    
 virājate sampati yuttiyutto 
 saddhammavaṃsādhivace nikāye 
 netuttamo kāruṇiko sasīla 
 kkhandhavhathero satimā vinīto 
  
    
 vibhāti vaṃse sumanavhanetu 
 pādassadānī garusaṅghanetā 
 saṅgepayaṃ sābhijanaṃ hi medhā 
 nandābhidhāno thaviro dhitīmā 
  
    
 yo sakkatādo nipuṇosi satthe 
 so gotamīkhyātavihāradhīso 
 sudhī yatindomaravaṃsathero 
 virājate viddasu matthakasmiṃ 
  
    
 viññātasatthāgamakosinoma 
 dassī mahānetuvaro vibhāvī 
 parakkamabbāhusamaññasatthā 
 layādhipo bhāsati sampatīha

 pāḷā̆ṇagāmamhi bhavo vibhāvī 
 susaṅkatho so vajirādiñāṇa 
 ssuto mahānetuvarojja bhāti 
  
    
 satthāgame chekataro susīlo 
 pasenathero matimā yatīso 
 vikhyātasaddhammudayākhyavijjā 
 layamhidhīso lasatejja sammā

 rāmādhipo netuvaro dayālū

 dhamme pavīṇo matimājja bhāti 
    sambhāvito sabbhi pasiddhavijjānandākhyavijjālayadhissaro hi 
 ñātāgamo sampati dhammasiddhi 
 yatissaro saṃlasate vibhāvī

 virājate so vidurūpolākhya

 bhūpassa āpañcamajōrjjanādhipaṃ 
 vuttantamasmiṃ itihāsikaṃ mahā 
 vaṃsamhi antogadhakaṅkarittha yo

 suvisadatatakittī sāsanabbhāradhārī

 tathariva mahataṃ konūtaresaṃ janānaṃ 
  
    
 iti viditajanā bho patthayantā hitatthaṃ 
 garukasiravighātaṃ niccasātaṃ paṇītaṃ 
 gamitumalasabhāvaṃ hitva tumheppamattā 
 cinutha cinutha puññā santataṃ santadampi 
  
 bhāṇavāramaṭṭha paññāsatimaṃ 
  
 iti sajjanānanda saṃvega janake dīpavaṃse punarajjamantana 
 sabhoccinanādi dīpano nāmaṭṭhapaññāsatimo paricchedo

 ekūnasaṭṭhitamo paricchedo  
  
   duṭṭhagāmiṇiabhayaraññā vikkamasālinā 
 tatodātasilokenasambuddhamāmakena hi

 vālutātitthagāmasmiṃsambhūtassa sivesino

 dīpavaṃsa dutiyaṃsa kattuvaṃso  
  
   sirighanamunino tilokakantā 
 riyatilakassakhilābhivanditena

   ativisadamahāvihāravaṃsā

 trajaviditagamamañjudhammapuñjo
